Current Commentary

The Issue of Restricting Foreign Rice Imports

— Liu

Regarding the two issues of restricting foreign rice imports and whether or not to increase taxes on No. 3 Saigon rice, although no conclusions were reached after the Executive Yuan convened a meeting to discuss them, they have already attracted widespread attention. Let us first discuss the first point, the restriction of foreign rice. Those who hold an opinion on this matter, from the perspective of farmers, fear that the continuous influx of foreign rice will depress the price of domestic rice, harming farmers. From the perspective of the people's food supply, they fear that once imports are restricted, rice merchants will manipulate the market, causing rice prices to skyrocket and leading to food shortages. Therefore, they are hesitant and unable to make a decision. As for the issue of whether or not to increase taxes on No. 3 Saigon rice, most people advocate for lower rice prices, arguing that taxation will make rice more expensive, which will hinder the people's food supply, and therefore oppose an increase. However, they do not consider the reasons for importing and taxing foreign rice, or whether or not taxes should be increased. They merely accuse rice merchants of profiteering, which only invites ridicule from the rice merchants themselves.

Originally, the issue of high or low grain prices is one of conflicting interests. Low grain prices hurt farmers, while high grain prices hurt the people. For three thousand years, this has been the common sentiment. Even the ever-normal granary system, while logical in theory, may not be entirely satisfactory in practice. Governing the law and governing the people are inherently difficult to reconcile. Therefore, discussing the people's food supply, especially in the current situation, is even more challenging to find a solution. However, one should not abandon the search for a solution simply because there is no easy answer. For example, what should be done with the large quantities of foreign rice currently in Shanghai? The central government is already considering this matter and will surely come up with a solution soon. Before this solution is revealed, let me briefly describe my own ideas.

Before discussing this issue, we must first examine the current rice prices in the city. Recently, rice prices have been quite stable and sluggish. However, the reasons for this stability and sluggishness, as far as I can surmise, are no more than: (1) The large quantities of foreign rice, mostly imported in March and April, require payment and delivery, causing a tight money supply. Merchants are forced to sell quickly to repay the import rice payments. This is due to the influx of foreign rice and the tight money supply. (2) Domestic rice that was stockpiled in previous years is difficult to store for long due to this year's tight money supply. If the rice is used as collateral for loans, it must be sold when the loan term expires. Thus, domestic rice is also sluggish. (3) The weather is gradually getting hotter. Although the mildew season is still far off, there is fear that the rice will spoil due to the heat, making it more advantageous to clear it out of the warehouses early. In addition to this, (4) there is also the psychological effect. Since the beginning of spring, the weather has been warm and there is hope for a good spring harvest. People fear that future rice prices will not be favorable. (5) The rural economy has been bankrupt for a long time. People cannot afford to buy rice when it is expensive, nor do they have the ability to buy it when it is cheap. Transactions are not as robust as in previous years, so stockpiles are growing thicker by the day, while sales are becoming increasingly sparse. Thus, rice prices are stable and sluggish. However, from the perspective of the people's food supply, stability and sluggishness are certainly a blessing. From the perspective of the market and finance, stockpiles are stagnant and there is no outlet. The money supply is bound to be strained. If there is any disturbance, the result will still be losses for domestic businesses, while foreigners will have already pocketed the profits. Therefore, even if there is an outlet for foreign rice, purchasing more foreign rice from an economic standpoint means paying more money to foreign countries, which is akin to drinking poison to quench thirst. If the outlet is not robust, then these 6 million dan of rice will still be a problem. If restrictions are not imposed and merchants are allowed to act freely, not only should we avoid purchasing more foreign goods under these circumstances to exacerbate the financial crisis, but we must also consider the future of our agricultural products and avoid increasing the pressure on them. Therefore, from the perspective of Shanghai alone, temporarily restricting the ordering of foreign rice would not be a bad idea.

However, how should we restrict the ordering? If restrictions are unsuccessful, what methods should be used to handle it? If restrictions are successful, but rice prices rise, what tactics should be used to stabilize them? These are questions that are indeed difficult to answer. Some say that it is not difficult, that the Social Affairs Bureau need only stop registering. But what kind of effect does the Social Affairs Bureau's registration have? It is merely intended to know the amount of rice entering and leaving the city, in order to regulate the market. If registration is stopped, can sales in the market be prohibited? Will customs not allow imports? No, it cannot. Therefore, the so-called stopping registration is merely a temporary measure taken in the absence of a better solution. It is not an effective method. Even if registration is stopped and sales are prohibited, it will only increase disputes and not solve the problem. Moreover, Shanghai is a place where Chinese and foreign merchants reside together, so the situation should be considered differently. Therefore, whether or not to register cannot restrict continued purchases. The only method is to advise merchants not to order anymore. But how can this be effective? If rice prices are stable and sluggish, merchants will not buy even without advice. If rice prices rise, although there is the threat of punishment, it will not outweigh their desire to profit, and they will inevitably try their luck. Moreover, foreign merchants aim to do business. If China needs it, they might as well raise prices to sell. If there is no need, they are willing to lower prices to sell. Therefore, if China's rice prices fall, foreign rice prices will also fall. When rice merchants see that the price of foreign rice is suitable for sale, they will inevitably order foreign rice. How can these rice merchants deeply consider the future consequences? They only know that the current profits are indeed substantial.

The method of advising has been exhausted. The most effective method is naturally to prohibit imports without registration, as advocated by some. However, prohibiting foreign rice imports should be implemented uniformly across the country, which is difficult to achieve. Guangdong relies on foreign rice for its supply. Xiang rice is prohibited from leaving the province. Anhui rice cannot be used. If foreign rice imports are prohibited, Guangdong will be plunged into a food crisis. From this, we can know that it is not feasible. If it is limited to the port of Shanghai, not only is it unreasonable, but how can we prevent foreign rice from being smuggled in? If the prohibitions are not uniform, how can we prevent it from being loaded and shipped? This is already so difficult from a domestic policy standpoint. As for foreign relations, can we be sure that it will not provoke criticism and cause disputes? We cannot be certain. Therefore, prohibiting foreign rice imports has its difficulties in today's world where customs rights are not yet complete. If diplomacy is successful, prohibition is possible and restriction is also possible. Neither would be a problem.

Before freely prohibiting its import, a more feasible method is the import permit system. Those who purchase foreign grain must obtain a passport. Customs releases goods based on the passport. When deemed unnecessary, the issuance of passports is stopped and imports cease naturally. When this system is implemented, it is necessary to understand the production of grain, the consumption of the people, and the supply and demand of the market. The difficulty still lies in whether or not prohibiting imports will cause additional problems. The difference is that there is no explicit prohibition of imports. It is only treated the same as military equipment and the like. Implementation seems easier. With this method, Guangdong and Shanghai can handle it separately. Guangdong can continue to issue passports, while Shanghai can stop issuing them. The foreign rice that has already been registered should be issued supplementary passports. If rice shortages still occur after the foreign rice is imported, continued issuance of passports can be considered to facilitate purchasing. Fortunately, once a telegram is sent for foreign rice, it can arrive in two weeks. At the same time, to prevent manipulation by rice merchants after purchases are stopped, a detailed investigation should be conducted on the numbers for rice in a certain region for arrival, sales, and inventory. The arrival, warehousing, sales, and destination of the licensed foreign rice, whether it is in the local or other ports, must be reported at any time for verification. Then, if rice merchants have a clear record of manipulating and hoarding, it will not be difficult to stop them. As for the issue of whether or not to increase taxes on No. 3 Saigon rice, due to space limitations, it will be discussed in another article.

U.S. Senator Opposes Participating in International Loans, Saying It Only Loses Friendship with Debtor Nations, Advocates Assisting China with Goods Instead of Cash

(Washington) Democratic Senator Lewis spoke in the Senate today, strongly opposing the United States' participation in international loans to China, saying that if the United States cooperates with other countries to provide China with financial assistance, the United States will be forced into a disadvantageous position. "Furthermore, we have painful experiences with lending to foreign countries. Not only are there monetary losses, but the friendship with the debtor nation is also lost. Therefore, if we want to avoid losing money and the friendship of the various countries involved in loans to China, it would be better to assist China by other means. We can suggest that if China needs loans, it may as well notify us in advance what it wants to purchase. If we can supply what it needs, we can supply it in full on credit," he said. According to reports, although congressmen have made many comments to the press about international loans to China, it is the first time that Louis has formally raised the issue on the floor of Congress. (National News Agency dispatch, 13th)

Germany Publicly Announces Reason for Establishing Air Force, Saying Britain, France, Russia, and the U.S. Are All Expanding Air Forces, France Studying Joint Action with Britain

(Berlin) The official foreign press agency today publicly stated for the first time that Germany has bomber planes. Yesterday, the German government announced that the German Air Force will be established on April 1st. Today, the foreign press agency said that the reason why Germany is re-establishing the air force is that Britain, France, Russia, and the U.S. have not only not abolished bombers, but have also formulated air force programs, modernized them in an organized manner, and improved bombers to make them play a decisive role in war. (Reuters dispatch, 13th)

(Paris) The German government notified Britain, France, and Italy, stating that Germany will formally organize an air force from April 1st of this year. This matter has caused many legal and diplomatic problems, which are currently being studied by the responsible personnel. It is investigated that this action by Germany, in addition to openly violating Part V of the Treaty of Versailles, also contradicts the Anglo-French London Declaration of February 3rd. Germany had previously accepted the London Declaration as the basis for negotiations. Now that the negotiations have not yet begun, Germany is taking the London Declaration's permission for Germany to participate in the Sky Convention as an excuse to establish an air force. However, the London Declaration clearly stipulates that the Sky Convention can only be signed after all the proposals of Britain and France have yielded results. Now that Germany has taken this action suddenly, there is no doubt that it violates the spirit of the London Declaration. It is now reported that the British and French governments have expressed their unity and will declare to Germany that all countries whose armaments are restricted by treaties have no right to unilaterally change their obligations. Germany cannot be regarded as an exception. In short, this declaration is nothing more than a reiteration of the claims announced in the Franco-Italian agreement of January 7th. In addition to the above legal issues, this move by Germany has also raised political issues in future negotiations. The governments of the countries concerned will naturally act together in accordance with the spirit of the Rome and London Agreements. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

Simon Scheduled to Visit Germany, Accompanying Eden on the 24th

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon is scheduled to travel to Berlin by plane with Lord Privy Seal Eden on March 24th to discuss everything with German leader Hitler on the 25th and 26th. It is reported that one of the issues to be discussed is recognizing Germany's re-establishment of the air force as legal, provided that Germany concludes a Sky Locarno Pact with Britain, France, Italy, and Belgium, an Eastern European Security Pact with Poland and the Soviet Union, and an Armaments Limitation Pact with various countries. Simon originally intended to travel alone, but the cabinet decided today that Eden should accompany him. In addition to serving as Lord Privy Seal, Eden is also a British disarmament expert, and the two travelling together will also make it seem more serious. According to reports, Simon was originally scheduled to go to Berlin on March 7th, but on March 5th, the day after Britain published its White Paper on National Defense, he received a letter from the German government stating that the leader was suffering from a cold and had lost his voice, and asked Simon to postpone his visit to Germany. Many believe that Germany was displeased with the White Paper's mention of Germany's rearmament and therefore took this action. The date of Simon's visit to Moscow is still under discussion with the Russian authorities and has not yet been decided. (Reuters dispatch, 13th)

(Berlin) Today's official gazette stated that German Foreign Minister Neurath informed the British ambassador last Saturday that Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to Berlin had been postponed due to leader Hitler's ill health. It can now be arranged within two weeks. The British ambassador suggested that March 25th or 26th be the travel date. The German government has now informed the British ambassador that it welcomes the British guest to arrive on that day. According to a London dispatch, Foreign Secretary Simon will be accompanied by Lord Privy Seal Eden, and is prepared to stay in Berlin for three days. However, it is still undecided whether Eden will go directly to Moscow from Berlin, as negotiations between Britain and Russia are still in progress. (National News Agency, 13th)

(Moscow) A Havas news agency correspondent in Moscow interviewed Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov, asking if it was true that the Soviet government had invited Eden to the Soviet Union, and if so, when would Eden arrive? Litvinov replied that when the Soviet government officially learned that the British government intended to send Eden to the Soviet Union, it immediately instructed its ambassador to inform the British Foreign Office that it would be very welcome for Mr. Eden to visit Moscow, and at the same time invited Mr. Eden to the Soviet capital. However, the date of Mr. Eden's departure has not yet been determined. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

(London) British cabinet members have now decided to go to Berlin on March 24th. British officials stated that the mission of the British cabinet members to Germany is to support the entire Anglo-French Joint Declaration of February 3rd. According to reports, there have recently been many malicious interpretations that the result of the British cabinet members' visit to Germany will cause the various key points in the Anglo-French proposal to be separated. This statement by officials refutes these interpretations. There are now various reasons to believe that Foreign Secretary Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden will be ordered to explain to Premier Hitler in detail that the British government believes that the issue of security in Eastern Europe and the issue of security in Germany's western border should not be separated. In other words, the British government regards all proposals advocating abandoning France and seeking an Eastern European security organization as out of step with the times. Therefore, the countries of Eastern Europe, Lithuania, Estonia, and Latvia, firmly believe that various instruments for preventing aggression must be interconnected. The London side is reportedly very pleased to hear this. Moreover, British diplomatic circles once believed that the Eastern European security organization could be based on the principle of non-interference in each other's internal affairs, but they no longer insist on this view, believing that only the provisions of mutual assistance can give the countries concerned a complete sense of security. Assuming, as hoped by the general public, that Germany approves the above principles and recognizes that the Eastern Pact cannot be separated from the issue of Western European security, the British representatives will continue to discuss with Germany, in proportion to the degree of satisfaction obtained in terms of security, and consider recognizing Germany's rearmament. However, in any case, there is a maximum limit to the recognition of Germany's rearmament, that is, it cannot be recognized that Germany has military power equal to that of the Soviet Union, because the Soviet Union's military power must cope with events in the Far East, and the danger on the Soviet Union's Far Eastern border is no less than that on its European border. In addition, well-informed sources believe that the recent order issued by the German government to transfer its civil aviation personnel to the military is a clear violation of Part V of the Treaty of Versailles. Before the British cabinet members went to Germany, this move by Germany was only a response to Britain's publication of the White Paper on National Defense policy, so it is not worth considering. However, upon reflection, the purpose of the Anglo-German talks is to conclude a new treaty to establish a security system. Now that these negotiations are about to begin, Germany is unilaterally abolishing the treaties it signed in the past, which is truly inconceivable. It is still unknown whether Britain will lodge a protest through diplomatic channels regarding Germany's establishment of an air force, or whether it will negotiate face-to-face when Simon goes to Germany. However, it is certain that Britain will not remain silent on this matter. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

British and French Parliaments Busy Discussing Military Affairs, Britain Building Fast Fighter Planes

(London) The Labour Party today moved a motion in the Upper House to impeach the government's national defense policy, but it was defeated. The mover, Lord Ponsonby, criticized the government's policy for increasing international disputes, causing an arms race, and hindering the progress of the disarmament conference. Secretary of State for War Hore-Belisha defended the government, saying that Britain's military strength only reached the minimum level necessary to protect the country, and the government would continue to base its policy on the League of Nations policy. Sassoon did not want to elaborate on the details of the plane, saying that it would not be convenient to do so for the public interest. Prospects for Naval Conference Dim as Countries Race to Expand Armaments

(Washington) Secretary of the Navy Swanson declared today that he believes it is "not very hopeful" for the establishment of an international agreement to limit the navy to replace the Washington Treaty. The Secretary of the Navy made this statement in response to a question as to whether France's intention to build a new 35,000-ton warship meant that an arms reduction treaty could no longer be established. Swanson said, "I still hope that it can be established again, but I am afraid that it is not very hopeful. It is now learned that both the United States and Britain are very willing to sign a new treaty before the Washington Treaty expires next year. At present, all countries are waiting for Japan to reopen the London Naval Talks. Spain's Five-Year Naval Plan

Madrid: Spain's five-year naval plan is about to be submitted to Congress. The contents have been disclosed in today's official gazette, including the construction of twelve submarines, each with a displacement of 400 tons; twelve torpedo boats, each with a displacement of 800 tons; eight mine sweepers; two torpedo boats; and twelve speedboats. Italy Actively Building Ships, Two New Cruisers Completed

(Rome) The new cruiser "Eugenio di Savoia" will be launched tomorrow in the port of Genoa. The new ship is of the same type as the "Condottieri", with a displacement of 7,000 tons, equipped with fourteen 152-mm guns, six torpedo tubes, and a speed of 30 knots per hour. There are also two cruisers of the same type under construction, which can be completed next year. In addition, Italy is also building (1) two 35,000-ton battleships, "Littorio" and "Vittorio Veneto"; (2) six destroyers; (3) five gunboats; and (4) five large and small submarines. The Italian Navy Department is studying various new plans. For example, the old cruiser "San Marco" will be abandoned within this year and used as a target for bombardment. At that time, the sailors on the ship will abandon ship and go ashore, and all changes in direction and speed will be controlled by radio. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

Greece Handles Those Who Betrayed the Party According to Law, More Than 300 People Subjected to Military Trial

Athens: The entire order in Greece has now been restored, and railway and telephone communications have been repaired. The reserves that were previously mobilized have also been demobilized. What the Greek government is now striving to do is to deal with the aftermath of the war and severely punish its political enemies according to law. Therefore, the original decree protecting the positions of judges and public officials has now been ordered to be suspended for three months, pending investigation by the government authorities into whether the existing officials have any suspicions of siding with the enemy. Various societies of the Venizelos faction are also strictly prohibited. Army Minister Kondylis has also declared that most of the seats in the Senate occupied by the Venizelos faction should be dissolved. A national assembly will be held in the next few days, at which time constitutional amendments such as the abolition of the Senate will also be submitted to the assembly for a vote. Senate Speaker Konatas has already been detained. In the past twenty-four hours, many people have been arrested on political charges, including Konatas. Army Minister Kondylis advocates that the leaders of the mutiny should be severely punished. There are about 300 people who should be subjected to military trial. As for the mutiny leader Venizelos himself, the government has stripped him of his citizenship and will be tried in absentia by the court. His property and that of other mutiny leaders will all be auctioned off and confiscated. Venizelos's former residence in Athens will henceforth be changed to the official residence of the mayor of Athens. In addition, a person named Pistotrakis, who is a relative of Venizelos, is said to have used his property to support the mutiny party, and has now also been arrested. (National News Agency dispatch, 13th)

The Future of Philippine Independence

(Washington) Since the delegation of Philippine Senate Speaker Quezon arrived in San Francisco, Washington is now anticipating that the preliminary plan to establish a Philippine Republic can be realized earlier. However, if the delegation requests to amend the Philippine Independence Act, there are still many questions about the future, as follows: (1) The delegation will accept the political provisions in the Independence Act, but hopes to amend the economic provisions. If the government cannot restore its prestige in the Senate, this move will not be easy. (2) It may request earlier independence and guaranteed reciprocal agreements. (3) Based on commercial equality, abandon the attempt for complete independence and seek a permanent relationship with the United States. US Bureau of Agriculture Director Gray told Associated Press reporters today that he had assured the Philippine delegation that he would cooperate in completing independence within three years, and after three years give the Philippines the treatment given to other countries. (National News Agency dispatch, 13th)

U.S. Army Tests Robot-Piloted Aircraft, New Weapons of Air Warfare Constantly Emerging

Oakland, USA: Today, a mysterious US Army aircraft, piloted by a robot, flew over the Pacific Ocean for three hours. According to official sources, the aircraft may "automatically" fly to Hawaii. The Army authorities are keeping this matter strictly secret, but it is learned that a number of officers were indeed on board during today's test flight, and may even fly to Honolulu on it. It is also reported that today's test flight was very successful. Observers said that if the Army can fly this mysterious aircraft from Oakland to Hawaii without human assistance, this move will be the greatest advance in the history of military aviation. In this case, if the United States encounters war, it can use this type of aircraft to drop bombs on enemy capitals without losing a single soldier. However, the Army has not yet admitted that robot flight has developed to this extent. It is said that the preparations for this test flight were very thorough, and the Hawaii flight is about to take place. The news reporters saw the plane add 1,600 gallons of gasoline, and the director of the Oakland airport ordered the Honolulu radio station to broadcast the letter E as a signal from 2:00 pm tomorrow. The plane should be able to receive the signal when it is 1,000 miles into the Pacific Ocean, and fly to the Honolulu Army Airfield according to the signal. The plane flew back today, at first thought to be due to machine failure, but it was later learned that this was a test flight to prepare for future long-range flights. It is said that today it flew 170 miles and has proven that flying to Hawaii is possible. The time of departure has not yet been announced, but the press believes that it may depart tomorrow afternoon. Those on board during today's test flight were Captains Hejink Bojer and Bisser, who are usually stationed in Honolulu. An Associated Press interviewer visited Karen to talk with the mother of Captain Bisser, who said that her son had been serving in Honolulu since September last year, but returned to Oakland on March 6th for secret affairs. (National News Agency dispatch, 13th)

(Washington) Following the announcement of the conversion of the Sunnyvale airship base into an aviation training station, there are now further proposals to Congress to study plans to strengthen California's coastal defense. Puppet Organization Issues Public Bonds to Raise Funds for Buying the Eastern Railway; Totaling 180 Million Yen; Japanese Banks Have Underwritten 30 Million

(Changchun) The "Manchukuo" today announced the public bond law for raising funds to buy the Chinese Eastern Railway. The main points are as follows: (1) In order to pay for the purchase of the Chinese Eastern Railway, public bonds in Japanese yen will be issued periodically, totaling 180 million yen. However, before issuing the bonds, funds equivalent to the issuance amount may be borrowed first. (2) These public bonds or pre-issuance loans are secured by the Chinese Eastern Railway and its income. (3) These public bonds or pre-issuance loans shall enjoy priority of repayment. (Hualian News Agency dispatch, 14th)

(Tokyo) Today at 11:00 a.m., representatives of the "Manchukuo" national bond banking group were received and a meeting was held at the Industrial Bank of Japan. As a result, the following unanimous agreement was reached:

Based on the basic contract, the first tranche of 30 million yen in "Manchukuo" public bonds, out of the total of 180 million yen for purchasing the North Manchuria Railway, will be accepted under the following conditions: (1) First issuance amount: 30 million yen; (1) Interest rate: 4%; (1) Issuance price: 98 yen; (1) Term: 10 years, with a fixed amount of 150,000 yen or more repaid every six months after three years; (1) Security: Railway property and its income; (1) Guarantee of principal and interest payment: A guarantee contract for the payment of principal and interest will be signed between the South Manchuria Railway and "Manchukuo"; (1) Issuance period: Early April; (1) Payment date: April 25. The Industrial Bank of Japan will sign on behalf of the banking group. Furthermore, at the time of signing the purchase of the North Manchuria Railway, the banking group will provide the "Manchukuo" government with a loan note of 21.33 million yen as a purchase fund, with a daily interest rate of 1.2%, which will be given to "Manchukuo" first and later exchanged for the issued public bonds. Nomura Securities will also participate in the banking group in the future. (Denstu News Agency dispatch, 14th)

British Pound Exchange Rate Rises

(London) The British pound rose today due to the revival of demand from Continental Europe. London financial newspapers all said that countries using gold are now on the verge of lowering their currency values. Today, the forward discount rate of the Belgian franc has increased from 0.55 centimes to 0.75 centimes. Although the [Dutch] guilder is still stable, the Belgian franc can be regarded as a very weak link, as Belgium's export difficulties are increasing rapidly. Only France can slightly reduce its difficulties, but if France wants to make concessions to Belgian industries, it will be greatly detrimental to its own trade. Switzerland is scheduled to hold a citizens' assembly on June 2 to decide on the country's future economic policy. It is said that its policy can easily become a devaluation of the currency through exchange restrictions. In many aspects, France also has a tendency to lower the price of the franc, but it is generally believed that the current rebound of the pound is temporary and will eventually fall, because the current price of the pound converted into US dollars is inevitably too high. Black Playwright Harrison Dies in New York

(New York) The famous black playwright Harrison died here today at the age of 70. Harrison was born in London and began his artistic career at the age of 25. He then traveled to the United States and Canada, and was famous for playing "God" in the play "The Green Pastures". He performed the play more than 800 times, including 640 times at the Mansfield Theater in New York. In 1930, he received the Spingarn Medal for the most outstanding achievement by a person of color. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

British Trade Continues to Improve

(London) According to the figures for February released today, British trade continues to improve. As a result, the optimism created by the British budget is becoming more intense. The total value of exports in February was £24,098,000, an increase of £4,038,000 compared to the same period last year. The total value of imports in February was £56,302,000, a decrease of £1,062,000 compared to the same month last year. Therefore, the trade deficit for January and February this year is only £39,100,000, compared to a trade deficit of £50,921,000 in the same period last year. Most of the increase in exports in February this year was in manufactured goods. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

All inherent virtues of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame all come from its source and are nurtured by it. (Xi'an) After completely eliminating scattered bandits in various important townships south of the Han River and the area near Mian County west of the Old River in southern Shaanxi, the bandit suppression focused on searching and suppressing bandits hiding in various mountains. After advancing in different directions, successive victories were achieved. All remnant bandits discovered have been cleared. The troops are continuing to search and suppress bandits in Ningqiang in the bandit area. Wang Yao Chen's regiment departed from Xishenba to clear the bandits. When they reached the vicinity of Niunaoke Ridge, they encountered more than 500 bandits. They launched a fierce attack and fought fiercely for three hours. The bandit forces could not hold out and fled south. In this battle, more than 100 bandits were killed and more than 80 guns were captured. The regiment is currently tracking and pursuing them. (Central News Agency dispatch, 14th)

Pacific Islands: US to Build Commercial Air Stations; Approved by Secretary of the Navy Swanson; Reserved for Military Use in Emergencies

(Washington) Pan American Airways, in preparation for establishing air transportation between Asia and the Americas, had planned to begin construction of airfields on Guam, Midway Island, and Wake Island in the Pacific next month. This plan has now been approved by Secretary of the Navy Swanson, but the government reserves the right to occupy these airfields in emergencies. (Havas, 13th)

(Washington) The Navy Department is today proceeding with assisting commercial organizations to install necessary equipment to open new Pacific air routes. International observers believe the Navy Department's approval of American Airlines' use of Midway Island, Wake Island, and Guam as bases for the Asia-America air route is intended to use them as a foundation for naval and military airfields in the future. It is said that, according to the Washington Treaty, the United States is not allowed to establish naval and military air bases on Midway Island, Wake Island, and Guam before 1936, but there are no restrictions on commercial airfields. It is learned that construction will be actively carried out on the islands to accommodate the takeoff and landing of large aircraft. A ship will depart from San Diego at the end of this month, fully loaded with materials, workers, and technicians. Because the islands are directly under the jurisdiction of the Navy Department, Secretary of the Navy Swanson has ordered the approval of the use of the islands, but the islands remain nominally under the Navy Department and can be immediately reclaimed from the airline in times of emergency. According to Pan American Airlines officials, the Asia-America air route will conduct its first test flight in mid-July. (National Telegram, 13th)

Japanese Navy's Perspective

(Tokyo) Japanese naval authorities are unwilling to comment on the news that the United States will turn Pacific islands into air bases, preparing them as powerful strongholds in case of emergency, and placing them under the control of the Navy Department. However, summarizing the opinions within the Navy Ministry, their view is as follows:

(1) The opening of air routes by the United States in its Pacific island territories, making them contact points for commercial air routes, and providing all necessary equipment, does not violate the treaty, even during the effective period of the Washington Treaty.

(1) However, the United States Navy Department, on the condition that it can transfer all commercial equipment to the Navy at any time and use it freely, is essentially disregarding the treaty by equipping civilian airlines. (1) It is difficult to understand why the United States is publishing such provocative news to Japan. If other countries do not disregard the treaty, no matter what facilities they have, we will not feel any pain or itch. No matter how they threaten, we will never yield. (1) We only hope that before the disarmament conference, all nations will strive to reach new agreements. Today, the United States' words of provocation to the world are unacceptable in a peace-loving America. (Dentsu Telegram, 14th)

Lu Dipin's Funeral Yesterday; Procession Stretched a Mile, Extremely Solemn

(Nanjing) Lu Dipin's funeral was held on the 14th. Important figures, military personnel, and military bands arrived one after another in the morning. At 8:05 AM, President Zhu of the Legislative Yuan also personally went to Lu's residence to pay respects at the mourning hall and left after ten minutes. At 8:30 AM, the coffin was raised amidst the sound of firecrackers and military music, which was extremely solemn. The funeral procession then departed from Baiziting, led by a name banner, followed by three hundred soldiers from the entire first regiment of the Training Corps, then the National Government Military Band, the National Government Commendation Pavilion, and the Inscription Pavilion. Lu's inscription was in front, inscribed by Wang, titled "General of the Army, Mr. Lu Yongan's Coffin." Sha's inscription was in the rear, inscribed by Lü Bichou, titled "Madam Sha, Mr. Lu's Concubine's Coffin." Next was the honor guard, the military band of the military department, incense pavilions, principal pavilions (Lu in front, Sha in the rear), the municipal band, flower garden teams, silver pagoda pavilions, ancient music, drum pavilions, the pallbearers Gu Zhenglun, He Yaozu, Chen Diaoyuan, and Yang Jie walked in front, followed by Dai Yue, Yue Sen, Chou Ao, Lü Bichou, and staff members of the Military Advisory Council, as well as more than three hundred relatives and friends of Lu. Next were mourners, then the coffin again, Lu's coffin in front, covered with a white flag with a blue sky and sun emblem, then a mourning shroud, carried by thirty-two porters. Sha's coffin followed behind. Behind the coffins were the family cars of the mourners, followed by the police department cavalry and thirty guards. The procession stretched for a mile. At 11:30 AM, they arrived at the Jinpu Railway ferry pier, where a special ship was moored to transport the coffins. The two coffins were moved onto the Jing'an Wheel one after the other and placed side by side in the lower deck of the large cabin, which was arranged as a mourning hall. The ship's sides were marked with large white banners reading "Special Ship for Transporting the Coffin of General of the Army Mr. Lu Yongan." The entire Lu family and about one hundred relatives and friends, along with a platoon of military police, accompanied the ship for protection. The ship was scheduled to set sail westward in the afternoon. Special envoys Chou Ao and Lu Dangping changed their flight to Hankou to the 16th. (Central News Agency, 14th)

(Nanjing) The Jing'an Wheel, carrying Lu Dipin's coffin, set sail westward at 4 PM on the 14th. Liu Zhenhua telegraphed on the 14th, planning to hold a memorial service on the Jianggan River in Anqing. He Jian also requested Chou Ao and Lu Dangping to return to Hunan as soon as possible to preside over the public memorial service. (Central News Agency, 14th)

International Commercial Telegram

Reuters Special Commercial News Telegram, March 14

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today is 147 shillings and 8 pence, 4 pence lower than yesterday.

London Silver Market: Today's spot price is 27.375 pence, up 0.0625. Futures are 27.4375 pence, the same as yesterday's price. The market situation is still stable. China bought, and India both bought and sold.

Mentally Ill Silver: Today's futures rose several pounds sterling.

Exchange Rates

British-American: Today, land purchases of British pounds, so the price of the British pound is in foreign currency, which has moved upward. The opening exchange rate between British and American currency was $4.74, 0.125 lower than yesterday's closing exchange rate. At 11:00 AM, it rose back to $4.748125. At 12:00 PM, it rose to $4.7575. At 2:00 PM in the afternoon, the price continued to rise to $4.76375, 2.375 higher than the opening.

British-French: The opening price was 71 francs 50, a pound lower than yesterday, but soon the price rose sharply. The latest price is 7 francs 06, 56 pounds higher than the opening.

American-British: In the New York foreign exchange market, the opening exchange rate for British currency was $4.75875, 1.75 higher. There were no changes afterwards. The opening price for French currency was $6.61, two pounds lower.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: The opening was relatively stable, with prices rising about 8 pounds. However, after the opening, prices fluctuated, falling back to yesterday's closing price. Public confidence in the cotton market is more stable than before, but it is prone to fluctuations. Senator Penhaid stated that although the Penhaid Act does not apply to cotton farmers with two bales, the number of ginned bales will not exceed 10.5 million bales as a result. After this statement was made, people's minds were slightly settled.

Chicago: Wheat received favorable weather news today. It is said that there has been no rain in areas that need rain, so the opening price rose slightly, but then fell slightly.

Liverpool Cotton: Today's situation is strong and stable. At 1:00 PM, the May futures price was 6.45, 7 pounds higher than yesterday.

Liverpool: The price is also relatively strong. The price of May futures rose by 3.75 to 4 shillings and 11.625 pence.

Rubber

London: Today's market situation is stable, but rather light. At noon, the transaction price for July-September futures was 6.1875 pence, 0.0625 higher than yesterday.

New York: Today's futures opened up 5 pounds and then fell back slightly.

Securities

New York: The unfavorable impact of the difficulties encountered by the authorities was reflected in the morale of Wall Street this morning. Before the opening, it was generally expected that securities prices would be low, but this was not the case. The opening prices of securities were mostly high. The average price of the Dow Jones 30 industrial stocks was 98.29, 27 pounds higher than yesterday. The market situation still has a slight upward trend, but transactions are not many and there is no hope of expansion. The market prices of New York securities are listed on the left:

Han River Steamer: Ran Aground and Destroyed off Daishan

First Mate Lost at Sea, Crew and Passengers Rescued; Steamer Worth 140,000 Yuan, Salvage Impossible

Xiamen Dispatch: The "Han River," a steamer belonging to the Xiamen Taili Steamship Company that plies the routes between Quanzhou, Shantou, and Wenzhou, set sail from Xiamen for Shantou. On the morning of the 6th, when it reached the mouth of Mayu Island in Shantou, it ran aground on a reef due to heavy fog at sea, which obscured its direction. It was immediately stuck and could not move. At the time, it was thought to be a minor issue, and it was planned to unload the cargo to lighten the ship and hopefully pull it off. However, the wind and waves were very strong, and the hull was tossed from side to side. The areas that hit the reef broke instantly. Before the cargo could be unloaded, the bow had already taken on water and sunk, leaving only the stern exposed in an inverted position. Subsequently, the engine room machinery was also damaged and flooded. At that time, four or five fishing boats saw the situation and came to rescue. In the confusion, the first mate, Hong Shizui, jumped into the sea. The shipowner asked the fishing boats to rescue him, but they were unsuccessful. His fate is currently unknown. When the Shantou Customs received the report, they immediately sent personnel on a motorboat to rescue. They first rescued the comprador Chen Shiji and Jiehe Company manager Ming Naishou and took them to Shantou. The remaining 80-plus passengers and crew were taken to Shantou on four fishing boats. The cargo, including paper umbrellas, was lost. When the Taili Company received the telegram, it sent the "Lujiang" steamer from Xiamen to inspect. It found that the "Han River" was aground on the reef and the hull and machinery were damaged beyond repair. The boilers had floated up and could not be towed back, so it sailed to Shantou and took some of the passengers (some remained in Shantou) and the crew back to Xiamen. The "Han River" had a purchase price of over 140,000 yuan and had been operating between Quanzhou, Shantou, and Wenzhou for nine years. The captain was Hong Lu, the first mate was Hong Shizui, the second mate was Cheng Binghui, the chief engineer was Wang Jisheng, the second engineer was Chen Jinquan, and the helmsman was Hong Longgong, and others. The entire crew consisted of 56 people, and there were 28 passengers. Except for Hong Shizui, all have been rescued. Hong was over 60 years old and had been the first mate on the Taili Company's "Jiankang" steamer for a long time. There is no possibility of salvaging the "Han River". (March 14)

Songjiang: Branch Bureau Chief Leaving Post Under Investigation

Li Ze, the chief of the Tinglin First Public Security Branch Bureau, allegedly released a morphine dealer. The Supervisory Committee of the Third District Party Department investigated the facts, obtained evidence from the detention book, and telegraphed the County Party Department to report the case. Upon hearing the news, Li first sent his family on the morning of the 9th, hiring a boat to Minhang and leaving. He also left the bureau that day and has not returned, leading to widespread rumors of desertion. Upon receiving the report, the Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched Detective Captain Yang Shijie to Hangzhou to arrest him, but to no avail. He has already returned to the bureau to report. Since Li's departure, Jiang Jiankang, the district chief of the Seventh District, has reported to the county government by phone, citing the lack of personnel to maintain local security and the importance of public security relations, requesting instructions. It is reported that the branch bureau is currently being temporarily maintained by Guan Jizhou.

Wuxi: Boats Traveling the Xiyu Route Robbed Mid-Journey

There has always been a cargo ship that travels between this city and Changshu, specializing in transporting goods for businesses in both cities. The boat owner is named Zhou Xufu, 29 years old, from Tangtou Town in the Fifth District of this city. At about 11 o'clock the afternoon before yesterday, the ship was fully loaded with goods, coming from Changshu to Wuxi. When it was sailing through the area inside Guan Bridge, north of Houqiao in the Seventh District of the county, suddenly more than 30 bandits, driving two small boats, each holding pistols, knives, clubs, and other weapons, sped towards them head-on. They swarmed onto the ship, forbidding anyone from making a sound, and searched at will. After about an hour, they plundered and fled towards Lujiatang. After checking the lost items, it was found that the boat owner lost more than 100 yuan in silver dollars, 13,000 copper coins, 80 bolts of cloth from the Changshu Xinfeng Cloth Factory, worth about more than 400 yuan, as well as a large pawn package from a certain pawnshop, half of which was opened, worth about more than 100 yuan, as well as clothing, resulting in significant losses. Zhou Xufu reported to the Houqiao Public Security Branch Bureau, which ordered Patrolman Li to go to the scene to investigate. Yesterday, the city's shipping association reported to the county government, requesting the arrest of the thieves.

Zhenjiang: Provincial Treasury Borrows 1.5 Million Yuan from Shanghai Banks

Since Zhao Dihua took office as the head of the provincial treasury, he has worked to rectify and reorganize the treasury. Although the province has suffered from rural bankruptcy and an unprecedented drought, causing a deficit in the provincial treasury, it has still managed to cope with various facilities and construction projects in the midst of extreme difficulties. However, the months of April, May, June, July, and August each year are lean seasons, with low tax revenue, while various provincial expenses cannot be delayed. Last April, the treasury mortgaged the province's business tax to the Shanghai banking community for 2 million yuan, which was repaid in monthly installments. It was fully repaid by February of this year. Now, the province is again mortgaging its business tax to the Shanghai branches of the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Jiangsu Provincial Bank for 1.5 million yuan, to be repaid in eight months, with interest rates remaining the same. A contract has been established. This loan is originally for the use of provincial expenses, so it has not yet been used.

Prodigal Son Returns Home in Glory

Han Yukang, the eldest son of Han Wanhe of Cu Lane, Xichenggen, was an apprentice in an oil mill, but he did not focus on his work and wandered around all day. He was fired for owing money. After returning home, he incurred debts of several hundred yuan due to gambling. His father sold property to repay the debts and expelled him, severing their father-son relationship. After being expelled in the autumn of 1923, Yukang regretted his actions too late. He went to Hankou to make a living, working hard and living frugally, abandoning his previous bad habits. In 1929, he raised funds to open his own oil company. His parents thought he was dead in a foreign land and burned paper money for him every festival, but Yukang never sent a letter home. At 6:00 last night, Yukang returned to Zhenjiang from Hankou with his wife and children because he missed his parents. When they arrived home, the whole family was overjoyed and reunited. This can be described as a prodigal son returning home is worth more than gold.

Huang Zhixiu, from Tianbu Township, Second District, served as a staff member of the Shanghai Municipal Party Department and a clerk in the Shanghai Municipal Government Wharf Management Office. She developed the idea of ​​despairing of the world and committed suicide by taking poison last night without anyone knowing. When the family discovered it, they called a doctor to rescue her, but it was ineffective, and she soon died.

City News

City Chamber of Commerce and Local Association Submit Proposal to Ministry of Finance: Contributing Credit Loan Measures

Requesting Government to Promote Banking Industry Support; Each Allocating 2.5 Million to Form Syndicate; Banking Association Already Approved in Principle

New Voice News Agency: The government and the banking industry are jointly launching a 5 million yuan industrial and commercial credit loan program. The City Chamber of Commerce and the Local Association submitted a proposal to the Ministry of Finance yesterday outlining measures for contributing to industrial and commercial credit loans. The Banking Association approved the principle at a meeting yesterday. The Money Exchange Association is scheduled to meet today to discuss the matter. The details are as follows:

Document from Chamber of Commerce and Local Association to Ministry of Finance

Submitted Regarding a Request: Your humble organizations, previously believing that the Shanghai market is tight and urgently needs relief, discussed and formulated five measures: (1) Various industry bills should be discounted by banks and money exchanges. If there is adequate collateral, the banks and money exchanges should accept them. The Central Bank should also provide rediscounting to the banks and money exchanges. (2) Land deeds and business licenses should be added as guaranteed reserves under the Central Bank's bond program. (3) Land deeds and business licenses, and store ledgers should be sent as usual. However, the amount of credit overdraft should be determined independently. (4) Three banks should accept goods or real estate as collateral for loans or bill discounts as much as possible. The above five measures have been sent to the Central Bank, the Savings Guarantee Reserve Committee, and the two Banking Associations for adoption and implementation. Regarding items two and three, we have also submitted a request to your ministry, requesting approval for implementation. On the 9th of this month, your humble organizations received two emergency relief plans for industry and commerce from China Industrial and Commercial Bank of this city. After detailed discussion, it was unanimously agreed that the second type of material property appraisal mortgage loan in its plan is actually item five of the measures proposed by your humble organizations. We have already sent letters to the Central Bank, Bank of Communications, and Three Banks, requesting that they accept these mortgages as much as possible. The first type of industrial and commercial small credit loan in its plan is also consistent with item four of the measures proposed by your humble organizations. However, if the government promotes relief to industry and commerce from above, and the banking industry assists from below, then mutual linkage will be more effective. After discussion, your humble organizations have further formulated four outline of small industrial and commercial credit loan measures as a supplement to item four of the proposed measures for implementation. We respectfully submit them again to your ministry for adoption and implementation. Industry and commerce will be fortunate. Respectfully submitted to the Minister of Finance.

Outline of Credit Loan Measures

The four outline of small industrial and commercial credit loan measures are as follows: (1) The applicant for the loan, directly or jointly with industry and commerce, should provide the name, total capital, business status, loan amount, and guarantor's name of the small loan applicant to the Chamber of Commerce and the Local Association for verification and registration, and then forward it to the syndicate jointly formed by the banking industry and the government. After review and approval, the designated representative bank of the syndicate will provide the loan. (2) The total amount of the loan is 5 million national currency, which is recognized by the government and the banking industry. (3) The amount guaranteed by the government is tentatively set at 2.5 million yuan. The Chamber of Commerce and the Local Association should submit a request to the Ministry of Finance for approval and allocation of funds. (4) All loan procedures are determined by the syndicate.

The Banking Association held its 62nd Standing Committee meeting and 64th Executive Committee meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday. In addition to the full attendance of all committee members, all member banks sent representatives to attend. After Chairman Chen Guangfu presided over the meeting and performed the rituals, Secretary-General Lin Kanghou read the resolutions of the previous meeting, and then began the discussion. (1) The Shanghai Local Association, for the purpose of jointly providing relief to industry and commerce, formulated an outline for small industrial and commercial credit loans and sent a letter requesting discussion and implementation. Attached is the letter from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce requesting that credit and mortgage loans be provided as usual as much as possible. Resolution: Approve in principle and organize a subcommittee. (2) The Beijing Banking Association believes that the new stamp tax law needs to be amended and sent a letter requesting consideration and handling. Resolution: Refer to the Banking Practices Committee for research. (3) The Shanghai Bank believes that for bank drafts with headers or horizontal lines, although there is no basis in the Negotiable Instruments Law, there is indeed such a custom and sent a letter requesting discussion and unified measures to be followed in order to strengthen security. Resolution: Refer to the Practices Committee for research. Temporary proposals: (1) Proposal from the Silk Industry Bank to accept drafts. Approve in principle and organize a subcommittee. The meeting adjourned at 3:00 PM.

The Money Exchange Association, regarding small industrial and commercial credit loans, has been decided by the Executive Committee to be submitted to the General Meeting of Members for a public decision. Yu Xuezhong Met with the Press Yesterday

Discussing War Zone Issues and Hebei Province's Finances; Touring Shanghai's Construction, Heading to Beijing Tomorrow Night

Central News Agency: Yu Xuezhong, Chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, he met with reporters from various newspapers at the Cangzhou Hotel. In the afternoon, he visited Mayor Wu at the Municipal Government and toured the construction of Greater Shanghai. He is scheduled to take the night train to Beijing today and then return north. When passing through Jinan, he decided to make a short stop to meet with Lu Province Chairman Han Fuqu. Yu's remarks are recorded as follows:

War Zone Issues

According to Yu, various issues within the North China war zone have gradually been resolved. The issue of the withdrawal of the Japanese and puppet troops from Malanyu will be resolved once Military Officer Takahashi returns to Ping from Changchun. The issue of the transfer of new and old security forces has been agreed upon, except for minor disputes over the number of personnel. The issue of the reorganization of the security forces has already begun. When Li Jichun's troops were pacified and reorganized, the number of troops under Zhao Lei was originally set at 2,000, and the number of troops under Liu Zuozhou was also set at 2,000. The number of troops pacified and reorganized under Shi Yousan was 1,000. Currently, the actual number of troops under Liu Zuozhou exceeds the original number by more than 300, and the actual number of troops under Shi Yousan also exceeds the original number by more than 800, resulting in a lack of supplies and occasional disturbances. Now, Feng Shoupeng's troops have been transferred to Tangshan, Sun Jizhou's troops have been transferred to the vicinity of Tongzhou, and Liu Zuozhou's troops have been transferred to Luanzhou to facilitate the dispatch of personnel from the War Zone Clearance Committee for strict reorganization.

Yellow River Breach

The current Yellow River breach is in a precarious situation. The largest breach is in Guantai, and the first to be affected is Hebei Province, followed by Shandong Province, and then Henan Province. Changyuan in Hebei Province has already been completely submerged, and Puyang has also been affected. This is because the dikes and breaches of the Yellow River are mostly repaired during the winter when the river is frozen. The weather was warm last winter, and the river did not freeze, making repairs difficult. In addition, spring floods caused this disaster. Currently, the Guantai breach is 26 meters deep and 26 meters wide, making it extremely difficult to block. The Water Conservancy Commission is currently working with the Hebei, Shandong, and Henan Provincial River Bureaus to discuss the aftermath.

Hebei Province's Finances

Since the September 18th Incident, Luandong has become a war zone, and tax revenues have sharply decreased. In addition, local wartime expenditures have doubled, resulting in a deficit of more than 6 million yuan. As of now, the debt is only more than 1 million yuan. It is expected that the old debts will be paid off in 1935, and the income and expenditures will offset each other. As for construction, progress is limited due to economic constraints. The future construction policy will focus on water conservancy and roads. The Lingshou Canal, built last year, cost more than 400,000 yuan and is expected to be completed this spring.

Provincial and City Boundary Demarcation

The issue of boundary demarcation between Beijing and Hebei Province has not yet been resolved. The area of Beijing was originally more than 2,000 square miles, the largest of all cities in the country. It is now planned to redraw the boundaries, expanding the area to more than 16,000 square miles. A boundary demarcation conference was held in Beijing once before, but there were no results, and it has not yet been resolved.

Huang Not Fully Recovered

Chairman Huang Yingbai's health is gradually improving, but he has not fully recovered. I visited the provincial government in Hangzhou this time. As for coming to Shanghai, it was also to visit the Shanghai municipal government to learn from it. I plan to leave Shanghai and return north tomorrow, and I will make a short stop in Jinan to see the recent situation in Shandong Province.

Gao Xibing Went to Hangzhou Yesterday; Returning to Shanghai in Four or Five Days and Transferring to Beijing

Gao Xibing, a member of the Xinjiang Provincial Government and Director of the Construction Department, went to Beijing to meet with the authorities and report on the recent situation in the new province. Yu Jichuan Discusses the Use of Hunan Province's Bonds

Two-Thirds for Building Roads, Rest for Repaying Old Debts; Finance Director Zhang Kailian May Arrive in Shanghai Tomorrow

National News Agency: Yu Jichuan, Director of the Construction Department of the Hunan Provincial Government, has been negotiating with the banking community in Shanghai on the mortgage of the province's construction bonds since his arrival in Shanghai on the morning of the 12th. The negotiations have been quite satisfactory. A reporter from the National News Agency met with Yu at his private residence yesterday and asked about the use of the bonds and the progress of the negotiations. Yu provided a detailed explanation.

Issued at 98

According to Yu, the total amount of the bonds is 10 million, which has been approved by the Legislative Yuan and allowed to be issued at 98 starting from January 1 this year, named the Hunan Provincial Construction Bonds of 1935. There are 15 articles in the regulations: (1) The Hunan Provincial Government will issue bonds worth 10 million yuan to build roads and repay old debts to banks, named the Hunan Provincial Construction Bonds of 1935. (2) The interest rate of the bonds is set at 6% per annum. (3) The bonds are issued at 98% of the face value. (4) The bonds are issued on January 1, 1935. (5) The bonds pay interest twice a year, on June 30 and December 31. (6) The bonds will be repaid using a lottery method starting on December 31, 1935, to be repaid over ten years. The lottery will be held twice a year until June 30, 1945, when all principal and interest will be fully repaid. The aforementioned lottery will be held annually on June 15 and December 15, and the payment will begin at the end of that month. The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Audit will send personnel to supervise each lottery. (7) The number of bonds to be drawn and the amount of principal to be repaid in each lottery are in accordance with the provisions of the attached table. (8) The Hunan Provincial Deed Tax and Business Tax revenues are the first guarantee for the bonds, and the operating income of the roads built with the bond funds is the second guarantee. The amount listed in the principal and interest repayment schedule will be allocated from the Hunan Provincial Deed Tax and Business Tax revenues on a regular basis as a fund for principal and interest repayment. (9) All income from the bonds and the principal and interest fund shall be stored in the agent national treasury and the provincial treasury banks. Representatives shall be appointed by the Administrative and Supervisory Yuan, the National Economic Council, the Hunan Provincial Finance and Construction Departments, the Banking Association, and the Provincial Chamber of Commerce to form a management committee to manage the funds. (10) The bonds are divided into four types: 10,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan, all of which are in unregistered form. (11) The agent national treasury and the provincial treasury banks are the agencies for managing principal and interest repayment. (12) Bonds drawn in the lottery and matured interest coupons can be used to pay all taxes in the province. (13) The bonds can be freely bought, sold, transferred, and mortgaged. They can be used as collateral when guarantee money must be paid for official affairs in the province and as collateral reserve funds for banks. (14) Those who forge bonds or damage credit will be punished by the judicial authorities in accordance with the law. (15) These regulations will take effect from the date of promulgation.

Use and Allocation

The bonds are currently being negotiated with the banking community in Shanghai, and the cash will be mortgaged at 60%. The use is determined to be two-thirds for the construction of the Xiangqian Highway and the remaining one-third for clearing the old debts of Xiang Province. They have already been printed and stored in the treasury for use. Interest will begin to be paid in June of this year, and principal will begin to be repaid on December 31, to be repaid over ten years until 1945. A fund management committee has been specially formed. The committee members are Liu Hongnian of the Executive Yuan, Tang Chuanming of the Ministry of Audit, Yang Silian of the Economic Council, Zhang Gongquan of the Banking Association (represented by Lu Yuexiang), Finance Director Zhang Kailian, Construction Director Yu Jichuan, and Tang Gan of the Provincial Chamber of Commerce, and was officially established in February. The first interest payment of 300,000 has been allocated by the Finance Department and deposited into the committee.

Signing the Contract

I (Yu said himself) have discussed this matter with the banking community several times, and there should be no problems in general. However, the interest rate, term, guarantee, etc. have not yet been determined. I plan to make a decision after Finance Director Zhang Kailian arrives in Shanghai. Zhang has already taken a ship from Hankou yesterday to Nanjing, landed and took an express train to Shanghai, and is expected to arrive tomorrow night. If the bond mortgage can be established, Zhang and I will sign it together.

National Federation of Chambers of Commerce Sends Telegram to Central Government Requesting Removal of Jiangxi Province's Timber Tax

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce telegraphed the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Industry yesterday, (omitted titles): Recently, we received a letter from the preparatory office of the Jingdezhen, Qimen, and other timber industry associations in Jiangxi, which roughly stated: In the 20th year of the Republic of China, the government, in consideration of the people's suffering, abolished the special timber tax. The timber industry benefited, and the dried fish awaited resuscitation. Not a year has passed, and the Jiangxi Provincial Government has reimposed a timber tax for production and sales to help with bandit suppression. At that time, merchants believed that this was a time-sensitive tax and, in order to support the government's plan to suppress bandits, they endured the pain of paying the tax, hoping for cooperation between the military and the people, without asking for its removal. Now that the bandits in Jiangxi Province have relied on the government's power to be suppressed and eliminated, this time-sensitive bandit suppression tax should naturally be abolished with the elimination of the bandits. Who knew that the hope of abolishing it had vanished, and an order to double the tax on January 1 of this year suddenly arrived. Merchants and hundreds of thousands of people along the borders of Jiangxi and Anhui provinces, who rely on this production as a source of livelihood, or rely on this work as a source of livelihood, will also be at a loss and await death. Therefore, merchants have telegraphed daily to the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Industry, earnestly requesting that the Jiangxi Provincial Government be ordered to immediately suspend the collection of this harsh and miscellaneous timber tax in order to emphasize production and restore construction. In response to this, we respectfully present this to your Yuan and departments for review and approval, earnestly requesting that you consider the difficulties of the people and quickly order the Jiangxi Provincial Government to suspend the collection of this timber tax in order to maintain the people's livelihood. Sincerely, Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, bows respectfully.

The Shenxin Seven Factories Incident: The Mystery of the Purchaser's Payment

The Key Lies Entirely in the Debt Repayment Issue: Rong Zongjing Says the Matter is in the Past

The Hua Dong News Agency reports that rumors have circulated about the purchaser of the Shenxin Seven Factories having made payment. A Hua Dong News Agency reporter revisited relevant parties yesterday morning to investigate. It is said that the aforementioned rumor is inaccurate. In fact, both the buyer and seller in this matter are part of the same organization. The key to resolving this issue lies entirely in the payment problem. Since this matter arose, after consistent negotiations from all levels of our government, HSBC has agreed to redeem the factories. However, they insist on full repayment of the principal and interest. Our side, after several discussions among Finance Minister Kong, Industry Minister Chen, Mayor Wu, and others, found that due to the circumstances, full repayment was realistically impossible. Therefore, they repeatedly negotiated with HSBC officials, proposing to first pay a portion of the interest, 250,000 yuan, and repay the rest in four installments. However, HSBC has consistently insisted on not allowing phased repayment. Until the deadline, the buyer falsely claimed that the payment had been cleared. Now, if our government agrees to HSBC's terms, redemption will no longer be an issue, it is said. Furthermore, sources have confirmed to Hua Dong News Agency reporters that no third party is involved in the turmoil. Since the Shenxin incident, people from all countries have been quite shocked, especially in this time of global economic recession. Although this sum of 2,250,000 yuan is small, in the eyes of most, the future business of the Shenxin Seven Factories cannot be managed as easily as it was under Mr. Rong Zongjing's management. Therefore, the current focus of resolution lies in the two issues of phased versus full repayment. As for the Shenxin side, up to now, they have not received any notification from any party. The factories are still operating as usual.

The Guowen News Agency reports that regarding the auction of the Shenxin Seven Factories, it has been rumored that the buyer has already made payment. Rong Zongjing told a Guowen News Agency reporter yesterday that the Shenxin Seven Factories were still operating yesterday. The auction issue is already in the past, and he hopes that the people of the country will not discuss it further. He only hopes that in the future, all compatriots will strive to use domestic goods and absolutely not buy foreign goods. On the one hand, he hopes that the government will implement the revival of rural areas, so that national cotton production will gradually increase. Then, Chinese-owned yarn factories will not need to purchase foreign cotton. If this is the case, the future of the yarn industry should be stable. As for the money owed to HSBC by the factories, part of the interest will be repaid first, and the principal will still be secured by the factory land and assets, it is said.

Cotton Control Association: Promoting Cotton Planting in Various Regions

Since its establishment, the Cotton Control Committee of the National Economic Commission has spared no effort in promoting the cotton industry in various regions. As a result, the cotton industry in various provinces has seen daily development. The committee estimates that within five years, it may no longer need to rely on foreign cotton. Recently, the Zhejiang Provincial Government, considering that the number of cotton planters in the province is increasing daily and the selection of cotton seeds is extremely important, entrusted the Cotton Control Committee to procure several thousand dan of cotton seeds. It is also reported that other provinces have also sent letters entrusting the committee to procure high-quality cotton seeds. It is expected that this year's cotton harvest will be much larger than last year's. To investigate the national cotton industry's conditions, the committee originally planned to send personnel to various regions every year for investigation. However, to save expenses and time, it has decided to adopt a communication-based survey.

The Cleaning Department of the Russo-Asiatic Bank Has Submitted a Lawsuit: Requesting the Seizure of the East, However, the Situation at the Wharf is Very Complex: It is Still Awaiting Court Approval

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that after the illegal sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway was realized, in addition to our government's protest and planned international statement, the Cleaning Department of the local Russo-Asiatic Bank has officially applied to the local court to execute the seizure of the East Railway's assets in Shanghai, such as the Pudong Wharf, because it has an interest in the railway. However, the wharf has been registered at the US Consulate, and the situation is quite complex. Details are noted below:

Application for Seizure

A few days ago, the reporter learned that the Cleaning Department of the Russo-Asiatic Bank had requested the court to seize the Yangjiadu Dong Railway Pudong Wharf and went to inquire. At that time, the spokesperson claimed that it was still under consideration, but yesterday it was no longer denied, proving that the application has indeed been submitted to the local court for execution, and entrusted to Chinese lawyers Yao Yongli and Yang Ruinian, and American lawyers Xu Li, Tai Weiss, and Lauton to handle everything. The reason for the request for seizure is that from October 1920 to the end of 1924, it had advanced funds to purchase railway materials, etc., totaling 589,637.52 yuan, but repeated demands for repayment have not been met. Now that the railway has been illegally sold, to protect its rights and interests, it has applied for execution of the seizure. However, according to the spokesperson of the bank, the court has not yet approved the application after the submission. However, the bank's legal advisor, Yawattendeski, believes that the legal basis for this action is quite solid.

Complex Relationships

However, the relationship of the wharf is quite complicated. According to reporter investigation, the wharf occupies 12 mu, 1 fen, 8 li, and 3 hao of land, with a width of 20 English feet, a riverfront of 450 English feet, a 300 English feet long pontoon, and a small warehouse and office. The total property value is 210,000 yuan. It is reported in the foreign press that it is worth 800,000 yuan, but the Russo-Asiatic Bank claims that it is not worth that much. It was registered at the US Consulate several years ago, with registration number 836. Therefore, it has actually become a four-way relationship among China, the United States, Japan, and Russia. Since Japan has declared that the Chinese Eastern Railway was purchased by a puppet state, Japan has no room to speak when the wharf is seized. Moreover, China has protested to Russia and declared to countries around the world that it does not recognize the illegal sale between Japan and Russia. Therefore, in law, China has the right to prevent the Soviet Union from transferring the wharf. However, since the United States is now involved, the problem is even more complex.
